 ship_secondaries_1 = {
	category = ship_secondaries
	sfx = sfx_ui_sd_module_turret
 
 
 
	add_stats = {
	   lg_attack = 1.5
	   build_cost_ic = 50
	}
	multiply_stats = {
	   naval_speed = -0.01
	}
	add_average_stats = {
	   lg_armor_piercing = 4.5
	}
	can_convert_from = {
	   module_category = ship_secondaries
	   convert_cost_ic = 45
	}
	critical parts = { damaged_secondaries }
 }
